```xml
            </GameItemTypeModelPack>
        </GameItemTypeArtDef>

```
_SOURCE: Clothing definitions (generated from xml/clothes/)_
# Clothing definitions (generated from xml/clothes/)

```
// Structure of documents
└── Mods/
    └── src/
        └── Data/
            └── GameCore/
```
